						<P CLASS="Texttable" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:0;orphans:1;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;text-align:right;"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">Filed Pursuant to Rule 424(b)(3)<BR></FONT><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">Registration No. 333</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">-289201</FONT></FONT></P>

		<P CLASS="H2" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:10pt;text-align:center;margin-top:10pt;"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;font-size:16pt;">Sui Group Holdings Limited</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="H2" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:10pt;text-align:center;margin-top:10pt;"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;">86,994,345&#x00a0;Shares of Common Stock</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">This prospectus relates to the potential offer and sale from time to time by A.G.P./Alliance Global Partners and its affiliates identified in this prospectus (collectively, &#x201c;A.G.P.&#x201d; or the &#x201c;Selling Stockholder&#x201d;) of up to 86,994,345<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of common stock of Sui Group Holdings Limited (&#x201c;we,&#x201d; &#x201c;us,&#x201d; &#x201c;our,&#x201d; the &#x201c;Company&#x201d; or &#x201c;SUIG&#x201d;), par value $0.001 per share (the &#x201c;Common Stock&#x201d;), that may be issued by us to the Selling Stockholder pursuant to that certain common stock purchase agreement, dated as of August&#x00a0;1, 2025, by and between the Company and the Selling Stockholder (the &#x201c;PEF Agreement&#x201d;), establishing a principal equity facility (&#x201c;PEF&#x201d;). The shares being offered for resale by this prospectus consist of Common Stock that we may, in our sole discretion, elect to issue and sell to the Selling Stockholder, from time to time after the date of this prospectus, pursuant to (and limited by the terms of) the PEF Agreement.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Pursuant to the terms of the PEF, we may elect, in our sole discretion, to issue and sell to the Selling Stockholder, from time to time, up to $500&#x00a0;million of shares of Common Stock (the &#x201c;Total Commitment&#x201d;) after the date of this prospectus. The shares of Common Stock will be purchased by the Selling Stockholder at a price per share equal to 95.0% of the volume weighted average price (&#x201c;VWAP&#x201d;) per share of our Common Stock, and equal to 95.0% of the VWAP for certain intraday purchases. As such, the actual number of shares of our Common Stock purchased by the Selling Stockholder under the PEF Agreement will vary depending on the then<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-current</FONT> market price of shares of our Common Stock sold to the Selling Stockholder under the PEF Agreement, but will not exceed the number set forth above unless we file an additional registration statement under the Securities Act&#x00a0;of&#x00a0;1933, as amended (the &#x201c;Securities Act&#x201d;), with the U.S.&#x00a0;Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#x201c;SEC&#x201d;). See &#x201c;<FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Prospectus Summary</FONT>&#x00a0;&#x2014;&#x00a0;<FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">PEF Agreement</FONT>&#x201d; and &#x201c;<FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">PEF Financing</FONT>&#x201d; for a description of the PEF Agreement and &#x201c;<FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Selling Stockholder</FONT>&#x201d; for additional information regarding the Selling Stockholder.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">We are not selling any securities under this prospectus and will not receive any proceeds from the sale of Common Stock by the Selling Stockholder pursuant to this prospectus. However, we may receive up to $500&#x00a0;million in aggregate gross proceeds from the Selling Stockholder under the PEF Agreement in connection with sales of the shares of our Common Stock we may elect to make pursuant to the PEF Agreement after the date of this prospectus. The actual proceeds received from the Selling Stockholder under the PEF Agreement may be less than this amount depending on the number of shares of our Common Stock sold and the price at which the shares of our Common Stock are sold. To the extent that the Company sells shares of Common Stock under the PEF Agreement, substantial amounts of shares could be issued and resold, which would cause dilution and may impact the Company&#x2019;s stock price. See &#x201c;<FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Risk Factors&#x00a0;&#x2014;</FONT>&#x00a0;<FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">The sale and issuance of our Common Stock to the Selling Stockholder will cause dilution to our existing stockholders, and the sale of the shares of Common Stock acquired by the Selling Stockholder and</FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">/</FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">or other stockholders, or the perception that such sales may occur, could cause the price of our Common Stock to decline</FONT>&#x201d; for additional information.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">A.G.P. is a registered broker<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-dealer</FONT> and FINRA member, and will act as an executing broker that will effectuate resales of our Common Stock that may be acquired by A.G.P. from us pursuant to the PEF Agreement to the public in this offering. Because A.G.P. will receive all the net proceeds from such resales of our Common Stock made to the public through A.G.P., A.G.P. is deemed to have a &#x201c;conflict of interest&#x201d; within the meaning of FINRA Rule&#x00a0;5121. Consequently, this offering will be conducted in compliance with the provisions of FINRA Rule&#x00a0;5121. Pursuant to that rule, the appointment of a &#x201c;qualified independent underwriter&#x201d; is not required in connection with this offering, as a &#x201c;bona fide public market,&#x201d; as defined in Rule&#x00a0;5121, exists for the securities offered.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The Selling Stockholder may sell or otherwise dispose of the shares of Common Stock described in this prospectus in a number of different ways and at varying prices. See &#x201c;<FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Plan of Distribution (Conflict of Interest)</FONT>&#x201d; for more information about how the Selling Stockholder may sell or otherwise dispose of such shares. Although the Selling Stockholder is obligated to purchase shares of our Common Stock under the terms of the PEF Agreement to the extent we choose to sell such Common Stock to them (subject to certain conditions), there can be no assurances that the Selling Stockholder will sell any or all of the shares of our Common Stock purchased under the PEF Agreement pursuant to this prospectus. A.G.P. is an &#x201c;underwriter&#x201d; within the meaning of Section&#x00a0;2(a)(11)&#x00a0;of the Securities Act&#x00a0;.</P>

		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">This summary highlights selected information contained in other parts of this prospectus. You should read the entire prospectus carefully, especially &#x201c;Risk Factors,&#x201d; &#x201c;Cautionary Note&#x00a0;Regarding </FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Forward</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">-Looking</FONT></FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;"> Statements and Industry Data,&#x201d; and our financial statements and the related notes incorporated by reference in this prospectus, before deciding to invest in shares of our Common Stock. 		<P CLASS="H2" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">Our Company</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Sui Group Holdings Limited is a Minnesota corporation that was incorporated in January&#x00a0;2006. From our inception until December&#x00a0;13, 2012, we were a development<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-stage</FONT> company involved in the gaming and entertainment industry. In 2013, we elected to become a business development company (&#x201c;BDC&#x201d;) under the Investment Company Act&#x00a0;of&#x00a0;1940 (the &#x201c;1940 Act&#x201d;). We operated as a BDC until we withdrew our BDC election on December&#x00a0;27, 2019. Since that time, we have engaged in the business of providing short<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-term</FONT> specialty finance solutions primarily to private businesses, micro- and small<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-cap</FONT> public companies and high<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-net</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak">-worth</FONT> individuals. To avoid again becoming subject to regulation under the 1940 Act, we generally seek to structure our short<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-term</FONT> loans such that they do not constitute &#x201c;securities&#x201d; under federal securities law, and we monitor our holdings as a whole to ensure that no more than 40% of our total assets may consist of &#x201c;investment securities,&#x201d; as that term is defined and understood under the 1940 Act.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Commencing July&#x00a0;27, 2025, the Company adopted a new treasury policy and strategy under which the principal holding in its treasury reserve on the balance sheet will be allocated to the native cryptocurrency of the Sui blockchain commonly referred to as &#x201c;SUI.&#x201d; The Board of Directors approved the Company&#x2019;s treasury policy on July&#x00a0;27, 2025, authorizing the long<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-term</FONT> accumulation of SUI.&#x00a0;We believe our position as a public company with an official Sui Foundation relationship through our the Digital Asset Purchase and Sale Agreement provides our investors with institutional<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-grade</FONT> exposure to the Sui blockchain, and that Sui is well positioned for large<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-scale</FONT> adoption with the speed and efficiency institutions require for crypto at scale, plus the technical architecture capable of supporting AI workloads while maintaining security and decentralization. The Sui Foundation is an independent organization dedicated to the advancement and adoption of the Sui network. The Company&#x2019;s approach involves acquiring SUI directly&#x00a0;&#x2014;&#x00a0;both through market purchases and direct purchases from the Sui Foundation. This treasury initiative seeks to enhance the Company&#x2019;s capital allocation strategy and does not affect its core commercial short<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-term</FONT> non<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-bank</FONT> lending and specialty finance business, which remains fully operational and a central part of the Company&#x2019;s business.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Effective August<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>26, 2025, we changed our corporate name from Mill City Ventures III, Ltd. to Sui Group Holdings Limited, and in connection with this change, the ticker symbol for the Common Stock on Nasdaq, and the ticker symbol for its common stock available for options trading on the Cboe, from &#x201c;MCVT&#x201d; to &#x201c;SUIG.&#x201d;</P>

	<DIV CLASS="BOXSTYLE" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;border-color:#000000;border-width:1pt;border: solid windowtext 1.0pt; padding: 10.0pt 4.0pt 10.0pt 4.0pt;">
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">herein shall be deemed to be modified or superseded for purposes of this prospectus to the extent that a statement contained herein or in any other subsequently filed document that also is or is deemed to be incorporated by reference herein modifies or replaces such statement. 		<P CLASS="H2" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">The PEF Agreement with A.G.P.</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">On August&#x00a0;1, 2025, we entered into the PEF Agreement with A.G.P. pursuant to which A.G.P. has agreed to purchase from us up to an aggregate of $500&#x00a0;million of our Common Stock (the &#x201c;Total Commitment&#x201d;) from time to time over the term of the PEF Agreement. Also, on August&#x00a0;1, 2025, we entered into a registration rights agreement with A.G.P. (the &#x201c;Registration Rights Agreement&#x201d;). Pursuant to our obligations under the Registration Rights Agreement, we have filed with the SEC the registration statement that includes this prospectus to register the resale under the Securities Act&#x00a0;of&#x00a0;the shares of Common Stock that may be issued to A.G.P. pursuant to the Total Commitment under the PEF Agreement.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">This prospectus covers the resale by the Selling Stockholder of an aggregate of 86,994,345<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of our Common Stock, comprised of&#x00a0;the shares we may issue and sell to A.G.P. as part of the Total Commitment in the future under the PEF Agreement.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">We do not have the right to commence any sales of our Common Stock to A.G.P. under the PEF Agreement until all of the conditions set forth in the PEF Agreement have been satisfied, including that the SEC has declared effective the registration statement that includes this prospectus registering the resale of the shares being issued and sold to A.G.P. under the Total Commitment (such date on which all of such conditions are satisfied, the &#x201c;Commencement Date&#x201d;). Thereafter, we may, from time to time and at our sole discretion for a period of 12&#x00a0;months from the Commencement Date, on any&#x00a0;trading&#x00a0;day that we select (so long as the time of delivery of such purchase notice is delivered in accordance with the PEF Agreement), direct A.G.P. to purchase up to the lesser of: (i)&#x00a0;the number of shares equal to not more than 25% of the total trading volume of the Common Stock during the applicable purchase valuation period and (ii)&#x00a0;$500,000 of shares of Common Stock.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">We will control the timing and amount of any sales of our Common Stock to A.G.P. under the PEF Agreement, but not the timing and amount of any subsequent resales by the Selling Stockholder. The purchase price of the shares that may be sold to A.G.P. in regular purchases under the PEF Agreement will be based on an agreed upon fixed discount to the market price of our Common Stock as computed pursuant to the terms of the PEF Agreement.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">We may at any time in our sole discretion terminate the PEF Agreement upon five&#x00a0;trading&#x00a0;days&#x2019; notice. There are no restrictions on future financings, rights of first refusal, participation rights, penalties or liquidated damages in the PEF Agreement or Registration Rights Agreement, except that we may not enter into any other &#x201c;equity line of credit&#x201d; or &#x201c;at the market offering&#x201d; or other substantially similar continuous offering during the term of the PEF.&#x00a0;Neither the Company nor A.G.P. may assign or transfer its rights and obligations under the PEF Agreement without the consent of the other party.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">If all of the 86,994,345<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of our Common Stock offered by A.G.P. under this prospectus were issued and outstanding as of the date hereof, such shares would represent approximately: (i)&#x00a0;51.5% of the total number of shares of our Common Stock outstanding and approximately 53.2% of the total number of outstanding shares of Common Stock held by non<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-affiliates</FONT> and (ii)&#x00a0;51.5% of the total voting power of all classes of our capital stock outstanding, in each case as of the date hereof. If we elect to issue and sell more than the 86,994,345<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares offered under this prospectus to A.G.P., which we have the right, but not the obligation, to do, we must first (i)&#x00a0;register the resale under the Securities Act&#x00a0;of&#x00a0;any such additional shares, which could cause additional substantial dilution to our stockholders, and (ii)&#x00a0;if applicable, obtain stockholder approval to issue shares of Common Stock in excess of the Exchange Cap (as defined below) under the PEF Agreement. The number of shares ultimately offered for resale by A.G.P. is dependent upon the number of shares we sell to A.G.P. under the PEF Agreement.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Under applicable rules&#x00a0;of the Nasdaq Capital Market, in no event may the Company issue or sell to A.G.P. under the PEF Agreement any shares of its Common Stock to the extent the issuance of such shares of Common Stock, when aggregated with all other shares of Common Stock issued pursuant to the ELOC Agreement, would cause the aggregate number of shares of Common Stock issued pursuant to the PEF Agreement to exceed 19.99% of the shares of all classes of our Common Stock outstanding immediately prior to the execution of the PEF Agreement (the &#x201c;Exchange Cap&#x201d;), unless (i)&#x00a0;the Company obtains stockholder approval to issue shares of Common Stock in </P>
		</DIV>

		<P CLASS="LRH" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:0;orphans:1;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:center;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin: 10px 0px 10px 0pt; page-break-after: always; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin-top: 10.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: 10.0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-align: center; font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: TimesNewRomanPSStd-Regular; color: black;">2</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:left;text-indent:0;widows:2;margin-top:8pt;"><A HREF="#TOC001">Table of Contents</A></P>






	<DIV CLASS="BOXSTYLE" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;border-color:#000000;border-width:1pt;border: solid windowtext 1.0pt; padding: 10.0pt 4.0pt 10.0pt 4.0pt;">
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">excess of the Exchange Cap or (ii)&#x00a0;the average price per share paid by the Selling Stockholder for all of the shares of Common Stock that we direct the Selling Stockholder to purchase from us pursuant to the PEF Agreement, if any, equals or exceeds the lower of (a)&#x00a0;the official closing price of our Common Stock on Nasdaq immediately preceding the execution of the PEF Agreement and (b)&#x00a0;the average official closing price of our Common Stock on Nasdaq for the five consecutive&#x00a0;trading&#x00a0;days immediately preceding the execution of the PEF Agreement, in either case so that the Exchange Cap limitation will not apply to issuances and sales of Common Stock pursuant to the PEF Agreement.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The PEF Agreement also prohibits us from directing A.G.P. to purchase any shares of Common Stock if those shares, when aggregated with all other shares of our Common Stock then beneficially owned by A.G.P. and its affiliates, would result in A.G.P. and its affiliates having beneficial ownership of more than 4.99% of the then total outstanding shares of our Common Stock, as calculated pursuant to Section&#x00a0;13(d)&#x00a0;the Exchange&#x00a0;Act, and Rule&#x00a0;13d<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-3</FONT> thereunder, which limitation we refer to as the &#x201c;Beneficial Ownership Cap.&#x201d; Notwithstanding the foregoing limitation, it would be possible for us to sell more than 4.99% of our outstanding shares of Common Stock to A.G.P. on any given&#x00a0;day if, during the course of such&#x00a0;day, A.G.P. sold the shares of Common Stock acquired by it such that it no longer owned 4.99% of our outstanding shares of Common Stock and we submitted, and A.G.P. accepted, an additional purchase notice; provided that, in no event, would A.G.P. own more than 4.99% of our outstanding shares of Common Stock at any one time.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The issuance of our shares of Common Stock to the Selling Stockholder pursuant to the PEF Agreement will not affect the rights or privileges of our existing stockholders, except that the economic and voting interests of each of our existing stockholders will be diluted as a result of any such issuance. Although the number of shares of Common Stock that our existing stockholders own will not decrease, the shares owned by our existing stockholders will represent a smaller&#x00a0;percentage of our total outstanding shares after any such issuance to A.G.P.. For more detailed information regarding the PEF Agreement, see the section entitled &#x201c;<FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">PEF Financing</FONT>.&#x201d;</P>
		<P CLASS="H2" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">Recent Developments</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="H3" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="BoldItalic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Change in Management</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Effective as of July&#x00a0;31, 2025, Lyle Berman resigned from the Board of Directors of the Company (the &#x201c;Board&#x201d;) and, to the extent applicable, all committees thereof. Mr.&#x00a0;Berman&#x2019;s resignation was not related to any disagreements with the Company.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">On July&#x00a0;27, 2025, and effective as of July&#x00a0;31, 2025, the Board elected and appointed Marius Barnett and Dana Wagner as members to the Board of the Company, to fill the vacancies on the Board. Mr.&#x00a0;Barnett is expected to serve as Chairman of the Board, and Mr.&#x00a0;Wagner is expected to serve on the Audit Committee of the Board.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">After such replacements, the Board will be composed of Douglas M.&#x00a0;Polinsky, Joseph A.&#x00a0;Geraci&#x00a0;II, Marius Barnett (chairman), Dana Wagner (independent), and Howard P.&#x00a0;Liszt (independent). The Audit Committee is composed of Mr.&#x00a0;Liszt and Mr.&#x00a0;Wagner. The Compensation Committee is composed of Mr.&#x00a0;Liszt. The Nominating and Corporate Governance Committee is composed of Mr.&#x00a0;Liszt.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">On July&#x00a0;27, 2025, and effective as of July&#x00a0;31, 2025, the Board made the following officer appointments:</P>
		<P CLASS="BL_m" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:48pt;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-24pt;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;"><FONT CLASS="bullet" STYLE="font-size:10pt;">&#x2022;<FONT STYLE="width: 27px;display: inline-block;">&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;</FONT></FONT>Stephen Mackintosh was appointed by the Board as the Chief Investment Officer of the Company. Mr.&#x00a0;Mackintosh, age<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>37, is a co<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-founder</FONT> at Karatage, a principal investing business in the blockchain and deep tech sector. He has also served as an advisor to the web3 cohort at Entrepreneurs First, a talent incubator that has helped create over 600 startups with a combined value of over $11&#x00a0;billion. Previously, Mr.&#x00a0;Mackintosh was Chief Commercial Officer at Re:infer, a natural language processing startup that was acquired by UiPath (NYSE:&#x00a0;PATH) in August&#x00a0;2022. He also served as an advisor to Resolve Group, a London<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-based</FONT> finance house providing corporate finance and restructuring services, acquired by Evelyn Partners. Mr.&#x00a0;Mackintosh earned a 1<FONT CLASS="CharOverride-2" STYLE="font-size:58%;vertical-align:super;">st</FONT> Class&#x00a0;BA Honors degree from University College London.</P>
		<P CLASS="H3" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="BoldItalic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">The SUI Strategy</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Commencing July&#x00a0;27, 2025, the Company adopted a new treasury policy and strategy under which the principal holding in its treasury reserve on the balance sheet will be allocated to the native cryptocurrency of the Sui blockchain commonly referred to as &#x201c;SUI.&#x201d; The Board of Directors approved the Company&#x2019;s treasury policy on July&#x00a0;27, 2025, </P>
		</DIV>

		<P CLASS="RRH" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:0;orphans:1;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:center;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin: 10px 0px 10px 0pt; page-break-after: always; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin-top: 10.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: 10.0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-align: center; font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: TimesNewRomanPSStd-Regular; color: black;">3</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:left;text-indent:0;widows:2;margin-top:8pt;"><A HREF="#TOC001">Table of Contents</A></P>






	<DIV CLASS="BOXSTYLE" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;border-color:#000000;border-width:1pt;border: solid windowtext 1.0pt; padding: 10.0pt 4.0pt 10.0pt 4.0pt;">
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">authorizing the long<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-term</FONT> accumulation of SUI.&#x00a0;We believe our position as a public company with an official Sui Foundation relationship through our the Digital Asset Purchase and Sale Agreement provides our investors with institutional<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-grade</FONT> exposure to the Sui blockchain, and that Sui is well positioned for large<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-scale</FONT> adoption with the speed and efficiency institutions require for crypto at scale, plus the technical architecture capable of supporting AI workloads while maintaining security and decentralization. The Sui Foundation is an independent organization dedicated to the advancement and adoption of the Sui network. The Company&#x2019;s approach involves acquiring SUI directly&#x00a0;&#x2014;&#x00a0;both through market purchases and direct purchases from the Sui Foundation. This treasury initiative seeks to enhance the Company&#x2019;s capital allocation strategy and does not affect its core commercial short<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-term</FONT> non<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-bank</FONT> lending and specialty finance business, which remains fully operational and a central part of the Company&#x2019;s business.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The Company raised gross proceeds of approximately $138<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>million in SUI (the &#x201c;SUI Proceeds&#x201d;) and approximately $312<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>million USD in cash (the &#x201c;Cash PIPE Proceeds&#x201d;) in the PIPE Transaction <FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">(see &#x201c;&#x2014; PIPE Transaction</FONT>&#x201d; below for additional information). On July<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>31, 2025, pursuant to the Digital Asset Purchase and Sale Agreement, the Company used approximately $140<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>million of the Cash PIPE Proceeds to acquire SUI (the &#x201c;Initial Purchased Digital Assets&#x201d;). <FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">See &#x201c;&#x2014; Digital Asset Purchase and Sale Agreement</FONT>&#x201d; below for additional information.) In the next 12<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>months, subject to market conditions, the Company intends to use approximately $140<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>million of Cash PIPE Proceeds to acquire additional SUI in the open market with the Asset Manager (Galaxy Digital Capital Management LP) as execution trader. Approximately 2% of the net proceeds from the PIPE Transaction will be used to fund the Company&#x2019;s short<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-term</FONT> lending business. The Company does currently intend to diversify its short<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-term</FONT> lending product offering or offer any new products in the next 12<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>months. <FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">See &#x2014; &#x201c;SUI Treasury Strategy</FONT>&#x201d; for additional information.</P>
		<P CLASS="H2" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;">Digital Asset Purchase and Sale Agreement</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">On July<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>27, 2025, the Company entered into a Digital Asset Purchase and Sale Agreement (the &#x201c;Digital Asset Purchase and Sale Agreement&#x201d;) with the Sui Foundation (the &#x201c;Foundation Investor&#x201d;), pursuant to which the Company agreed to purchase and the Foundation Investor agreed to sell and transfer a certain number of SUI tokens equal to one half of the aggregate cash proceeds of the PIPE Transaction (as defined below), calculated in accordance with the procedures set out in the Digital Asset Purchase and Sale Agreement (the &#x201c;Initial Purchase Amount&#x201d;). The price per SUI token purchased pursuant to the Initial Purchase Amount was equal to the product of (i) 0.85 multiplied by (ii) the twenty<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-four</FONT> (24)<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-hour</FONT> time weighted average price on July<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>31, 2025, i.e., the date on which the PIPE Transaction closed (the &#x201c;Closing Date&#x201d;), as reasonably calculated by the Company. From and after the Closing Date, until such time as the aggregate amount of all completed Subsequent Purchases (as defined below) equals the Initial Purchase Amount, the Company will allocate one half of all cash raised by the Company subsequent to the PIPE Transaction (whether through additional sales of equity interests or otherwise) to offer to purchase additional SUI tokens from the Foundation Investor (each, a &#x201d;Subsequent Purchase&#x201d;). The price per SUI token purchased pursuant to any such Subsequent Purchase shall be equal to the product of (i) 0.85 multiplied by (ii) the twenty four (24)<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-hour</FONT> time weighted average price on the relevant date), as reasonably calculated by the Company. The Digital Asset Purchase and Sale Agreement also provides the Company with certain preemptive rights, including the right to purchase up to 20% of SUI tokens proposed to be sold by the Foundation Investor in any over<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-the-counter</FONT> sale with gross proceeds exceeding $50,000,000 for a two (2) year period after the Closing Date. Pursuant to the terms of the Digital Asset Purchase and Sale Agreement, the SUI tokens purchased will be subject to transfer restrictions for a period of two (2) years following the Closing Date. Notwithstanding the foregoing, the transfer restrictions will not apply to the extent necessary to enable the Company to comply, or to be in compliance with, the provisions of the U.S. Investment Company Act of 1940. </P>
		<P CLASS="H3" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="BoldItalic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">PIPE Transaction</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">On July&#x00a0;27, 2025, the Company entered into securities purchase agreements (the &#x201c;Securities Purchase Agreements&#x201d;) with the investors identified on the signature pages thereto (the &#x201c;PIPE Investors&#x201d;) and a related registration rights agreement (the &#x201c;RRA&#x201d;) in connection with the issuance and sale in a private placement of the following securities to the PIPE Investors for gross proceeds of approximately $450&#x00a0;million: (i)&#x00a0;75,881,625<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares (the &#x201c;Common Shares&#x201d;) of the Company&#x2019;s Common Stock and (ii)&#x00a0;pre<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-funded</FONT> warrants (the &#x201c;Pre<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-Funded</FONT> Warrants&#x201d;) to purchase up to an aggregate of 7,144,205<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock (the &#x201c;Pre<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-Funded</FONT> Warrant Shares&#x201d;) at an exercise price of $0.0001 per share (the &#x201c;PIPE Transaction&#x201d;). The offering price for one share of Common Stock was $5.42 and the offering price for one Pre<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-Funded</FONT> Warrant was $5.4199.&#x00a0;The PIPE Transaction closed on July&#x00a0;31, 2025.</P>
		</DIV>

		<P CLASS="LRH" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:0;orphans:1;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:center;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin: 10px 0px 10px 0pt; page-break-after: always; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin-top: 10.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: 10.0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-align: center; font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: TimesNewRomanPSStd-Regular; color: black;">4</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:left;text-indent:0;widows:2;margin-top:8pt;"><A HREF="#TOC001">Table of Contents</A></P>






	<DIV CLASS="BOXSTYLE" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;border-color:#000000;border-width:1pt;border: solid windowtext 1.0pt; padding: 10.0pt 4.0pt 10.0pt 4.0pt;">
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The Pre<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-Funded</FONT> Warrants are exercisable immediately, and may be exercised at any time until all of the Pre<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-Funded</FONT> Warrants issued in the PIPE transaction are exercised in full. The exercise price and number of Pre<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-Funded</FONT> Warrant Shares issuable upon exercise of the Pre<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-Funded</FONT> Warrant are subject to appropriate adjustment in the event of stock dividends, stock splits, reorganizations or similar events affecting our Common Stock and the exercise price. The Pre<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-Funded</FONT> Warrant may be exercised, in whole or in part, at any time by means of a &#x201c;cashless exercise.&#x201d; The Pre<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-Funded</FONT> Warrants for certain PIPE Investors provide that the holder may not exercise any portion of such holder&#x2019;s Pre<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-Funded</FONT> Warrants to the extent that the holder, together with its affiliates, would beneficially own more than 4.99% (or, at the election of the holder, 9.99%) of the Company&#x2019;s outstanding shares of Common Stock immediately after exercise, except that upon at least 61&#x00a0;days&#x2019; prior notice from the holder to the Company, the holder may increase the beneficial ownership limitation to up to 19.99% of the number of shares of Common Stock outstanding immediately after giving effect to the exercise.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Pursuant to the Securities Purchase Agreements, the Company has agreed not to issue, enter into any agreement to issue, or announce the issuance or proposed issuance of any shares of Common Stock or Common Stock equivalents, or file any registration statement or any amendment or supplement thereto, for a period of 15&#x00a0;days after the effective date of the Resale Registration Statement (as defined below), subject to certain customary exceptions. The Company also agreed not to undertake any reclassifications of its Common Stock, such as a reverse or forward stock split, without the written consent of PIPE Investors holding a majority in interest of the shares issued or issuable to each PIPE Investor under the Securities Purchase Agreements, for a period of one year following the closing of the PIPE Transaction, provided such consent will not be required to conduct a reverse stock split to maintain listing of the Common Stock on The Nasdaq Capital Market.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The Company intends to use the proceeds from the PIPE Transaction to acquire the native cryptocurrency of the Sui blockchain commonly referred to as &#x201c;SUI&#x201d; and other cryptocurrencies with the Sui layer 1 blockchain protocol and for the establishment of the Company&#x2019;s cryptocurrency treasury operations, with 2% of the net proceeds to be used to fund the Company&#x2019;s short<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-term</FONT> lending business.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Additionally, pursuant to the Securities Purchase Agreements, the Company issued:</P>
		<P CLASS="NL_m" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:48pt;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-24pt;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">(i)<FONT STYLE="width: 17px;display: inline-block;">&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;</FONT>warrants (the &#x201c;Lead Investor Warrants&#x201d;) to Karatage Opportunities (&#x201c;Karatage&#x201d;), a Purchaser in the PIPE transaction and a strategic advisor to the Company (as described below), to purchase 3,113,469<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock (the &#x201c;Lead Investor Warrant Shares&#x201d;) at various prices per share of Common Stock as follows: (i)&#x00a0;1,245,387<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock at an exercise price of $5.42 per share of Common Stock; (ii)&#x00a0;1,245,387<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock at an exercise price of $5.962 per share of Common Stock; (iii)&#x00a0;415,129<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock at an exercise price of $6.504 per share of Common Stock; and (iv)&#x00a0;207,565<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock at an exercise price of $7.046 per share of Common Stock;</P>
		<P CLASS="NL_m" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:48pt;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-24pt;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">(ii)<FONT STYLE="width: 13px;display: inline-block;">&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;</FONT>warrants (the &#x201c;Foundation Investor Warrants&#x201d;) to the Sui Foundation (the &#x201c;Foundation Investor&#x201d;), a Purchaser in the PIPE transaction, to purchase 3,113,469<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock (the &#x201c;Foundation Investor Warrant Shares&#x201d;) at various prices per share of Common Stock as follows: (i)&#x00a0;1,245,387<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock at an exercise price of $5.42 per share of Common Stock; (ii)&#x00a0;1,245,387<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock at an exercise price of $5.962 per share of Common Stock; (iii)&#x00a0;415,129<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock at an exercise price of $6.504 per share of Common Stock; and (iv)&#x00a0;207,565<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock at an exercise price of $7.046 per share of Common Stock;</P>
		<P CLASS="NL_m" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:48pt;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-24pt;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">(iii)<FONT STYLE="width: 10px;display: inline-block;">&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;</FONT>warrants (the &#x201c;Management Warrants&#x201d;) to certain members of the management of the Company to purchase 1,245,387<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock (the &#x201c;Management Warrant Shares&#x201d;) at various prices per share of Common Stock as follows: (i)&#x00a0;622,694<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock at an exercise price of $5.42 per share of Common Stock; (ii)&#x00a0;415,129<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock at an exercise price of $6.504 per share of Common Stock; and (iii)&#x00a0;207,565<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock at an exercise price of $7.046 per share of Common Stock; and</P>
		<P CLASS="NL_m" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:48pt;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-24pt;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">(iv)<FONT STYLE="width: 10px;display: inline-block;">&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;</FONT>warrants (the &#x201c;Advisor Warrants&#x201d; and together with the Lead Investor Warrants, the Foundation Investor Warrants and the Management Warrants, the &#x201c;Warrants&#x201d;) to certain advisors of the Company to purchase 207,565<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock (the &#x201c;Advisor Warrant Shares&#x201d; and together with the Lead Investor Warrant Shares, the Foundation Investor Warrant Shares and the Management Warrant Shares, the &#x201c;Warrant Shares&#x201d;) at a price per share equal to $5.962.</P>

		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:left;text-indent:0;widows:2;margin-top:8pt;"><A HREF="#TOC001">Table of Contents</A></P>






	<DIV CLASS="BOXSTYLE" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;border-color:#000000;border-width:1pt;border: solid windowtext 1.0pt; padding: 10.0pt 4.0pt 10.0pt 4.0pt;">
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The Warrants are exercisable for a period of five&#x00a0;years from the date of issuance of the Warrants. The Warrants will vest over a period of 24&#x00a0;months starting six&#x00a0;months from the Issue Date (as defined therein) in four equal installments (being 25% every six&#x00a0;months) and in the case of the Management Warrants, subject to the relevant holder still being employed by the Company at each respective vesting date. Notwithstanding the foregoing, in the event that member of the management team is terminated by the Company other than for cause or resigns for good reason (as defined in the individual&#x2019;s employment agreement), the vesting of all of such individual&#x2019;s Management Warrants will immediately accelerate and be fully vested as of the date of such termination.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Under the RRA entered into in connection with the PIPE Transaction, the Company agreed to file a registration statement (the &#x201c;Resale Registration Statement&#x201d;) for the resale by the PIPE Investors of the Common Shares, the Pre<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-Funded</FONT> Warrant Shares, Lead Investor Warrant Shares, Foundation Investor Warrant Shares and Management Warrant Shares within 10&#x00a0;days of the closing of the PIPE Transaction under the Securities Purchase Agreements, and to have the registration statement declared effective within 30&#x00a0;days of its filing date, subject to certain exceptions.</P>

		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">As of September<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>16, 2025, we had 82,148,429<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock issued and outstanding. Additional information regarding our issued and outstanding securities may be found under &#x201c;<FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Description of Capital Stock</FONT>.&#x201d;</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Unless otherwise specifically stated, information throughout this prospectus does not assume the exercise of outstanding options or warrants to purchase shares of our Common Stock and gives effect to the Stock Split.</P>
		<P CLASS="H2" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">Implications of Being a Smaller Reporting Company</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">We are a &#x201c;smaller reporting company&#x201d; as defined in Item&#x00a0;10(f)(1)&#x00a0;of Regulation&#x00a0;S<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-K</FONT>, and have elected to take advantage of certain of the scaled disclosure available for smaller reporting companies. We will remain a smaller reporting company until the end of the fiscal year in which (1)&#x00a0;we have a public common equity float of more than $250&#x00a0;million, or (2)&#x00a0;we have annual revenues for the most recently completed fiscal year of more than $100&#x00a0;million and a public common equity float or public float of more than $700&#x00a0;million. We also would not be eligible for status as a smaller reporting company if we become an investment company, an asset<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-backed</FONT> issuer or a majority<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-owned</FONT> subsidiary of a parent company that is not a smaller reporting company.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">We have elected to take advantage of certain of the reduced disclosure obligations in the registration statement of which this prospectus is a part and may elect to take advantage of other reduced reporting requirements in future filings. As a result, the information that we provide to our stockholders may be different from what you might receive from other public reporting companies in which you hold equity interests.</P>

The actual proceeds from the Selling Stockholder may be less than this amount depending on the number of shares of our Common Stock sold to the Selling Stockholder and the price at which such shares are sold. The purchase price per share that the Selling Stockholder will pay for shares of Common Stock purchased from us under the PEF Agreement will fluctuate based on the market price of our shares at the time we elect to sell shares to the Selling Stockholder and, further, to the extent that the Company sells shares of Common Stock under the PEF Agreement, substantial amounts of shares could be issued and resold, which would cause dilution and may impact the Company&#x2019;s stock price. 		<P CLASS="H1" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:1;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:center;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><A NAME="T9"></A><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">RISK FACTORS</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Investing in our securities involves a high degree of risk. You should carefully consider the risks and uncertainties described under &#x201c;Risk Factors&#x201d; in our most recent annual report on Form&#x00a0;10</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">-K</FONT></FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;"> as supplemented or updated in our most recent quarterly report on Form&#x00a0;10</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">-Q</FONT></FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">, any current report on Form&#x00a0;8</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">-K</FONT></FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">, as well as any accompanying prospectus supplement, together with all of the other information included or incorporated by reference in this prospectus and in any accompanying prospectus supplement, including our financial statements and related notes, before deciding whether to purchase our securities.</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Our business, financial condition and results of operations could be materially and adversely affected by any or all of these risks or by additional risks and uncertainties not presently known to us or that we currently deem immaterial that may adversely affect us in the future. The Company is supplementing the risk factors previously disclosed in its Annual Report on Form&#x00a0;10</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">-K</FONT></FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;"> for the year ended December&#x00a0;31, 2024, as amended (the &#x201c;Form&#x00a0;10</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">-K</FONT></FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">&#x201d;) with the following risk factors. These risk factors should be read in conjunction with the risk factors included in the Form&#x00a0;10</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">-K</FONT></FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">.</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="H2" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">Risks Related to This Offering and Ownership of Our Common Stock</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="H3" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="BoldItalic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">It is not possible to predict the actual number of shares of our Common Stock, if any, we will sell under the PEF Agreement, or the actual gross proceeds resulting from those sales or the dilution to you from those sales. Further, our inability to access a part or all of the amount available under the PEF Agreement, in the absence of any other financing sources, could have a material adverse effect on our business.</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Pursuant to the PEF Agreement, the Selling Stockholder has committed to purchase up to $500&#x00a0;million of shares of Common Stock from us, subject to certain limitation and conditions set forth in the PEF Agreement. The shares of our Common Stock that may be issued under the PEF Agreement may be sold by us to the Selling Stockholder at our discretion from time to time over a 12<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-month</FONT> period from the date of the PEF Agreement, commencing after the satisfaction of certain conditions set forth in the PEF Agreement, including that the SEC has declared effective the registration statement that includes this prospectus.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">We generally have the right to control the timing and amount of any sales of our Common Stock to the Selling Stockholder under the PEF Agreement. Sales of our Common Stock, if any, to the Selling Stockholder under the PEF Agreement will depend upon market conditions and other factors to be determined by us. We may ultimately decide to sell to the Selling Stockholder all, some or none of the Common Stock that may be available for us to sell pursuant to the PEF Agreement.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Because the purchase price per share of Common Stock to be paid by the Selling Stockholder for the Common Stock that we may elect to sell to the Selling Stockholder under the PEF Agreement, if any, will fluctuate based on the market prices of our Common Stock at the time we make such election, it is not possible for us to predict, as of the date of this prospectus and prior to any such sales, the number of shares of Common Stock that we will sell to the Selling Stockholder under the PEF Agreement, the purchase price per share that the Selling Stockholder will pay for the shares of Common Stock purchased from us under the PEF Agreement, or the aggregate gross proceeds that we will receive from those purchases by the Selling Stockholder under the PEF Agreement, if any.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The Selling Stockholder can resell, under this prospectus, up to 86,994,345<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock, which is approximately 1.06 times as many shares as the 82,148,429<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock we currently have outstanding. If all of the 86,994,345<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of our Common Stock shares offered by the Selling Stockholder under this prospectus were issued and outstanding as of the date hereof, such shares would represent approximately: (i)&#x00a0;51.4% of the total number of shares of our Common Stock outstanding and approximately 53.1% of the total number of outstanding shares of Common Stock held by non<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-affiliates</FONT> and (ii)&#x00a0;51.4% of the total voting power of all classes of our capital stock outstanding, in each case as of the date hereof. Even if we elect to sell to the Selling Stockholder all of the 86,994,345<FONT CLASS="nobreak"> </FONT>shares of Common Stock being registered for resale under this prospectus, depending on the market price of our Common Stock at the time we elect to sell shares to the Selling Stockholder pursuant to the PEF Agreement, the actual gross proceeds from the sale of all such shares may be substantially less than the amount available to us under the PEF Agreement, which could materially and adversely affect our liquidity position. Further, if we are unable to access all or a portion of the amount available under the PEF Agreement to meet our liquidity needs, we may be required to seek other financing sources and utilize more costly and time<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-consuming</FONT> means of accessing the capital markets, which could have a material adverse effect on our business, liquidity and cash position.</P>
