For example, an NFT may convey rights to a digital asset that exists in an online game or a decentralized app, and users can trade their NFT in the decentralized app or game, and carry them to other digital experiences, creating an entirely new free<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-market</FONT> internet<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-native</FONT> economy that can be monetized in the physical world.</P>
		<P CLASS="H4" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:1;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Overview of the Sui Network&#x2019;s Operations</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">In order to own, transfer or use SUI directly on the Sui Network (as opposed to through an intermediary, such as a custodian), a person generally must have internet access to connect to the Sui Network. SUI transactions may be made directly between end<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-users</FONT> without the need for a third<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-party</FONT> intermediary. The Sui Network prevents double<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-spending</FONT> by validating and recording transactions either through direct validator execution or, when needed, via consensus. Transactions involving shared objects are memorialized on the Sui blockchain to ensure consistency and prevent conflicts. This verification process is managed by validators who either directly execute transactions or reach consensus to include shared<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-object</FONT> transactions in checkpointed blocks. These blocks form part of the Sui blockchain, which acts as a source of truth for shared state. Unlike traditional blockchains that rely solely on the sequential production of blocks for all transactions, the Sui Network differentiates between independent and shared transactions. Independent transactions can be executed in parallel without global ordering, while only shared transactions require consensus and block inclusion.</P>
		<P CLASS="H2" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">SUI Token Issuance</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="H4" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:1;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Initial Creation of SUI and SUI Supply</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Unlike Bitcoin, which was solely created through a progressive mining process, 10&#x00a0;billion SUI were created in connection with the launch of the Sui Network. Following the launch of the Sui Network, no further SUI will be created unless a modification (or &#x201c;fork&#x201d;) of the Sui Network&#x2019;s protocol occurs. The Sui Network&#x2019;s capped total supply of 10&#x00a0;billion SUI tokens are unlocked according to a distribution and unlock schedule designed to balance liquidity, stability, and long<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-term</FONT> growth. The current unlock schedule is subject to adjustments to ensure a stable tokenomics model that supports the Sui Network&#x2019;s health and will be available for download via an API maintained by the Sui Foundation. According to the Sui Foundation, distributions of locked SUI tokens were made to Series&#x00a0;A and Series&#x00a0;B investors and early contributors beginning in April&#x00a0;2024, and distributions of locked SUI tokens were made to Mysten Labs Treasury beginning in October&#x00a0;2023.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The Sui &#x201c;mainnet&#x201d; launched on May&#x00a0;3, 2023 with a portion of the total supply made liquid at launch. At or shortly after launch, the mainnet was supported by over 100 validators and over 400 nodes. DeepBook, the Sui Network&#x2019;s first native liquidity layer, launched in July&#x00a0;2023. This central limit order book gives DeFi protocols and other app builders a mechanism to support both market and limit token swaps. By mid<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-July</FONT>&#x00a0;2023, the Sui Network had approximately one million active wallets, rising to approximately three million active wallets by mid<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-August</FONT>&#x00a0;2023, nine million active wallets by the end of November&#x00a0;2023, and over 120&#x00a0;million active wallets by mid<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-April</FONT>&#x00a0;2025.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">On September&#x00a0;13, 2023, zkLogin, a new primitive, launched on the Sui Network, letting builders incorporate authorization through existing credentials from providers such as Google, Facebook and Twitch. This development significantly eased the onboarding path for new Web3 users.</P>
		</DIV>

		<P CLASS="RRH" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:0;orphans:1;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:center;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin: 10px 0px 10px 0pt; page-break-after: always; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin-top: 10.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: 10.0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-align: center; font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: TimesNewRomanPSStd-Regular; color: black;">36</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:left;text-indent:0;widows:2;margin-top:8pt;"><A HREF="#TOC001">Table of Contents</A></P>



	<DIV CLASS="_idGenObjectStyleOverride-1" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;border-width:0pt;">
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">By February&#x00a0;2024, DeFi protocols on the Sui Network had reached $500&#x00a0;million in total value locked, putting the Sui Network in the top ten blockchains by that metric. That number rose to $1&#x00a0;billion in total value locked by the end of September&#x00a0;2024, and $2&#x00a0;billion in January&#x00a0;2025. By April&#x00a0;2024, the beta version of the 2024 edition of the Move programming language became available, which added many useful new features, including method syntax, positional fields, and loop labels. On June&#x00a0;18, 2024, Mysten Labs announced the launch of Walrus, a decentralized data storage network that uses SUI as a coordination layer. Walrus launched on the Sui Network in April&#x00a0;2025.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">On August&#x00a0;6, 2024, engineers launched Mysticeti, a new consensus mechanism for the Sui Network that could allow the Sui Network to process shared object transactions with even less latency. In September&#x00a0;2024, Agora&#x2019;s U.S.&#x00a0;dollar<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-backed</FONT> stablecoin arrived on the Sui Network, giving DeFi users a new option for token purchases and swaps. The advent of AUSD on the Sui Network, which was previously launched on Ethereum and Avalanche, was one of a number of native stablecoins on the Sui Network. Sui USDC, which is the SUI<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-native</FONT> version of USDC, another stablecoin, was added to the Sui Network in October&#x00a0;2024, and FDUSD, yet another stablecoin, was added to the Sui Network in November&#x00a0;2024.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The SUI token serves four purposes on the Sui Network. First, SUI can be staked within an &#x201c;epoch&#x201d; in order to participate in the proof<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-of</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak">-stake</FONT> mechanism. Second, SUI is the asset denomination needed for paying the Gas Fees to execute transactions or other operations on the Sui Network. Third, SUI can be used as a versatile and liquid asset for various applications including the standard features of money&#x00a0;&#x2014;&#x00a0;a unit of account, a medium of exchange, or a store of value&#x00a0;&#x2014;&#x00a0;and more complex functionality enabled by smart contracts, interoperability, and composability across the Sui ecosystem. Fourth, and finally, SUI plays an important role in governance by acting as a right to participate in on<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-chain</FONT> voting on issues such as protocol upgrades.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The SUI token powers a variety of real<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-world</FONT> applications:</P>
		<P CLASS="NL_m" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:48pt;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-24pt;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">1.<FONT STYLE="width: 20px;display: inline-block;">&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;</FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Decentralized Finance</FONT>:&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;Lending and borrowing protocols allow users to supply SUI for interest or borrow against collateral. Yield farming and staking rewards allow liquidity providers to earn yield by participating in automated market makers and liquidity pools. Stablecoins and payments benefit from SUI&#x2019;s fast and low<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-cost</FONT> transactions, making it ideal for cross<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-border</FONT> transfers and remittances.</P>
		<P CLASS="NL_m" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:48pt;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-24pt;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">2.<FONT STYLE="width: 20px;display: inline-block;">&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;</FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Non</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">-Fungible</FONT></FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;"> Tokens</FONT>:&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;NFT minting and trading allow artists and developers to create and trade NFTs on SUI&#x2019;s blockchain with low minting costs. On<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-chain</FONT> gaming assets enable in<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-game</FONT> items, skins, and collectibles to be represented as NFTs, unlocking true ownership.</P>
		<P CLASS="NL_m" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:48pt;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-24pt;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">3.<FONT STYLE="width: 20px;display: inline-block;">&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;</FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Gaming and Metaverse</FONT>:&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;Play<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-to</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak">-earn</FONT> gaming economies allow players to earn rewards in a decentralized manner. Low<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-latency</FONT> transactions enable smooth in<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-game</FONT> purchases and seamless on<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-chain</FONT> interactions.</P>
		<P CLASS="NL_m" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:48pt;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-24pt;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">4.<FONT STYLE="width: 20px;display: inline-block;">&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;</FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Supply Chain and Enterprise Solutions</FONT>:&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;Provenance and authentication solutions track goods transparently, ensuring authenticity and reducing fraud. Enterprise blockchain integration supports identity management, record<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-keeping</FONT>, and automation.</P>
		<P CLASS="NL_m" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:48pt;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-24pt;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">5.<FONT STYLE="width: 20px;display: inline-block;">&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;</FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Identity Verification and Security</FONT>:&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;Decentralized identity solutions verify credentials and prevent fraud. Data privacy enhancements allow privacy<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-preserving</FONT> transactions and selective disclosure mechanisms.</P>
		<P CLASS="H4" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:1;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Limits on SUI Supply</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">SUI has a fixed total supply of 10&#x00a0;billion tokens, meaning no additional SUI will be minted beyond this limit. At network launch, a portion of the total supply was in circulation, while the remaining tokens are being released progressively over time. The structured emission schedule is designed to support network security, incentivize validators and participants, and sustain the long<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-term</FONT> growth of the Sui Network. Additionally, pursuant to the Digital Asset Purchase and Sale Agreement, the Initial Purchased Digital Assets (approximately 45% of the Company&#x2019;s SUI holdings) are subject to a lock<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-up</FONT> period of thirty (30) days after the two<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-year</FONT> anniversary of the closing date of the PIPE Transaction.</P>
		<P CLASS="H2" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">Governance of the Sui Network and Modifications to the Protocol</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">SUI token holders participate in network governance by voting on protocol upgrades, fee adjustments, and validator policies and incentives. The governance model is designed to be inclusive and transparent, encouraging community<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-driven</FONT> decision<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-making</FONT>.</P>
		</DIV>

		<P CLASS="LRH" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:0;orphans:1;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:center;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin: 10px 0px 10px 0pt; page-break-after: always; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin-top: 10.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: 10.0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-align: center; font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: TimesNewRomanPSStd-Regular; color: black;">37</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:left;text-indent:0;widows:2;margin-top:8pt;"><A HREF="#TOC001">Table of Contents</A></P>



	<DIV CLASS="_idGenObjectStyleOverride-1" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;border-width:0pt;">
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The Sui Foundation oversees ecosystem development, distributing funds for grants, research, and innovation to drive network growth. The Sui Foundation is an independent, non<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-profit</FONT> entity established to support and advance the adoption, security, and sustainability of the Sui Network. The Sui Foundation is dedicated to fostering an open ecosystem that empowers developers, users, and enterprises to build and interact with blockchain<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-based</FONT> applications. As the primary steward of the Sui Network, it plays a pivotal role in the protocol&#x2019;s long<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-term</FONT> development by overseeing ecosystem growth, allocating community resources, funding research initiatives, and ensuring governance transparency. The Sui Foundation operates in alignment with the principles of decentralization, innovation, and inclusivity, promoting an equitable and sustainable blockchain ecosystem.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The core development team behind the Sui Network is Mysten, a blockchain technology company focused on developing innovative and scalable solutions to enhance decentralized applications and blockchain infrastructure. Mysten played a foundational role in designing and launching the Sui Network. The company continues to contribute to SUI&#x2019;s technical advancements while fostering an ecosystem of developers, enterprises, and users who leverage its cutting<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-edge</FONT> infrastructure. Mysten operates as a private technology company and is distinct from the Sui Foundation, which oversees governance, community funding, and decentralization efforts for the Sui Network. While Mysten remains a significant contributor, the long<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-term</FONT> evolution of SUI is guided by decentralized governance mechanisms and community participation.</P>
		<P CLASS="H2" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">Summary of a SUI Transaction</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The following is a summary of a payment transaction of SUI on the Sui Network.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Prior to engaging in SUI transactions directly on the Sui Network, a user generally must first install on its computer or mobile device a Sui Network software program that will allow the user to generate a private and public key pair associated with a SUI address. The Sui Network software program and the SUI address also enable the user to connect to the Sui Network and transfer SUI to, and receive SUI from, other users.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Each Sui Network address, or wallet, is associated with a unique &#x201c;public key&#x201d; and &#x201c;private key&#x201d; pair. To receive SUI, the SUI recipient must provide its public key to the party initiating the transfer. This activity is analogous to a recipient for a transaction in U.S.&#x00a0;dollars providing a routing address in wire instructions to the payor so that cash may be wired to the recipient&#x2019;s account. The payor approves the transfer to the address provided by the recipient by &#x201c;signing&#x201d; a transaction that consists of the recipient&#x2019;s public key with the private key of the address from where the payor is transferring the SUI.&#x00a0;The recipient, however, does not make public or provide to the sender its related private key. Wallets that are used to store cryptographic keys can be &#x201c;hot&#x201d; or &#x201c;cold.&#x201d; A hot wallet is connected to the internet, and is thus readily available to facilitate trading, but may be more vulnerable to hacking. A cold wallet is a wallet that stores cryptographic keys offline, such as on a computer that has no internet access, a segregated piece of hardware, or a piece of paper.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Neither the recipient nor the sender reveal their private keys in a transaction, because the private key authorizes transfer of the funds in that address to other users. Therefore, if a user loses his or her private key, the user may permanently lose access to the SUI contained in the associated address. Likewise, SUI is irretrievably lost if the private key associated with them is deleted and no backup has been made. When sending SUI, a user&#x2019;s Sui Network software program must validate the transaction with the associated private key. In addition, since every computation on the Sui Network requires processing power, there is a transaction fee involved with the transfer that is paid by the payor. The resulting digitally validated transaction is sent by the user&#x2019;s Sui Network software program to the Sui Network validators to allow transaction confirmation.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Sui Network validators record and confirm transactions when they validate and add blocks of information to the Sui Blockchain. When a validator validates transactions, it creates a block, which includes data relating to (i)&#x00a0;the verification of newly submitted and accepted transactions and (ii)&#x00a0;a reference to transactions prior to the transactions is being added. The validator becomes aware of outstanding, unrecorded transactions through the data packet transmission and distribution discussed above.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Upon the addition of a block of SUI transactions, the Sui Network software program of both the spending party and the receiving party will show confirmation of the transaction on the Sui Blockchain and reflect an adjustment to the SUI balance in each party&#x2019;s Sui Network public key, completing the SUI transaction. Once a transaction is confirmed on the Sui Blockchain, it is irreversible.</P>
		</DIV>

		<P CLASS="RRH" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:0;orphans:1;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:center;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin: 10px 0px 10px 0pt; page-break-after: always; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin-top: 10.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: 10.0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-align: center; font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: TimesNewRomanPSStd-Regular; color: black;">38</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:left;text-indent:0;widows:2;margin-top:8pt;"><A HREF="#TOC001">Table of Contents</A></P>



	<DIV CLASS="_idGenObjectStyleOverride-1" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;border-width:0pt;">
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Some SUI transactions are conducted &#x201c;off<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-blockchain</FONT>&#x201d; and are therefore not recorded in the Sui Blockchain. These &#x201c;off<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-blockchain</FONT> transactions&#x201d; involve the transfer of control over, or ownership of, a specific digital wallet holding SUI or the reallocation of ownership of certain SUI in a pooled<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-ownership</FONT> digital wallet, such as a digital wallet owned by a Digital Asset Trading Platform. In contrast to on<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-blockchain</FONT> transactions, which are publicly recorded on the Sui Blockchain, information and data regarding off<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-blockchain</FONT> transactions are generally not publicly available. Therefore, off<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-blockchain</FONT> transactions are not truly Sui transactions in that they do not involve the transfer of transaction data on the Sui Network and do not reflect a movement of SUI between addresses recorded on the Sui Network&#x2019;s blockchain. For these reasons, off<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-blockchain</FONT> transactions are subject to risks as any such transfer of SUI ownership is not protected by the protocol behind the Sui Network or recorded in, and validated through, the blockchain mechanism.</P>
		<P CLASS="H2" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">SUI Markets and Exchanges</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">SUI can be transferred in direct peer<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-to</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak">-peer</FONT> transactions through the direct sending of SUI over the Sui Network from one Sui Network address to another.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">SUI can be used as a means to conduct cross<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-border</FONT> payments and to pay other users of the Sui Network for goods and services under what resembles a barter system. Consumers can also pay merchants and other commercial businesses for goods or services through direct peer<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-to</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak">-peer</FONT> transactions on the Sui Network or through third<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-party</FONT> service providers.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">In addition to using SUI to engage in cross<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-border</FONT> transactions or payment for goods and services, investors may purchase and sell SUI to speculate as to the price of SUI in the SUI market, or as a long<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-term</FONT> investment to diversify their portfolio. The price of SUI within the market is determined, in part, by the supply of and demand for SUI in the global SUI market, market expectations for the adoption of SUI as a store of value or as a viable cross<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-border</FONT> payments facilitator, the number of merchants that accept SUI, the regulatory challenges faced by SUI, and the volume of peer<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-to</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak">-peer</FONT> transactions, among other factors.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">SUI spot markets typically permit investors to open accounts with the market and then purchase and sell SUI via websites or through mobile applications. Prices for trades on SUI spot markets are typically reported publicly. An investor opening a trading account on a digital asset trading platform must deposit an accepted government<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-issued</FONT> currency into its account with the trading platform, or a previously acquired digital asset, before they can purchase or sell assets on the trading platform. The process of establishing an account with a digital asset trading platform and trading SUI is different from, and should not be confused with, the process of users sending SUI from one SUI address to another SUI address on the Sui Network. This latter process is an activity that occurs on the Sui Network, while the former is an activity that occurs entirely within the order book operated by the digital asset trading platform. The digital asset trading platform typically records the investor&#x2019;s ownership of SUI in its internal books and records, rather than on the Sui Network. The digital asset trading platform ordinarily does not transfer SUI to the investor on the Sui Network unless the investor makes a request to the exchange to withdraw the SUI in its platform trading account to an off<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-platform</FONT> SUI wallet.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Outside of the spot markets, SUI can be traded SUI.&#x00a0;The SUI market is largely institutional in nature, and SUI market participants generally consist of institutional entities, such as firms that offer two<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-sided</FONT> liquidity for SUI, investment managers, proprietary trading firms, high<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-net</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak">-worth</FONT> individuals that trade SUI on a proprietary basis, entities with sizeable SUI holdings, and family offices. The SUI market provides a relatively flexible market in terms of quotes, price, quantity, and other factors, although it tends to involve large blocks of SUI.&#x00a0;The SUI market has no formal structure and no open<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-outcry</FONT> meeting place. Parties engaging in OTC transactions will agree upon a price&#x00a0;&#x2014;&#x00a0;often via phone or email&#x00a0;&#x2014;&#x00a0;and then one of the two parties will then initiate the transaction. For example, a seller of SUI could initiate the transaction by sending the SUI to the buyer&#x2019;s SUI address. The buyer would then wire U.S.&#x00a0;dollars to the seller&#x2019;s bank account. OTC trades are sometimes hedged and eventually settled with concomitant trades on digital asset trading platforms.</P>
		<P CLASS="H2" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">SUI Token Circulation</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Newly created SUI are generated through a process referred to as &#x201c;staking&#x201d; which is when an actor on the Sui Network acquires SUI and then pledges that SUI as collateral. This collateral is then put at risk in exchange for the validator collecting rewards for services rendered to the Sui Network in the process of forming consensus and adding blocks to the blockchain. When the recipient makes newly minted SUI available for sale, there can be downward pressure on the price of SUI as the new supply is introduced into the SUI market.</P>
		</DIV>

		<P CLASS="LRH" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:0;orphans:1;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:center;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin: 10px 0px 10px 0pt; page-break-after: always; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin-top: 10.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: 10.0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-align: center; font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: TimesNewRomanPSStd-Regular; color: black;">39</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:left;text-indent:0;widows:2;margin-top:8pt;"><A HREF="#TOC001">Table of Contents</A></P>



	<DIV CLASS="_idGenObjectStyleOverride-1" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;border-width:0pt;">
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The Sui Network contains several deflationary measures. The total number of SUI that can ever be created is capped at 10&#x00a0;billion. Because the supply of SUI is capped, increased activity on the network has a deflationary effect as the Sui Network&#x2019;s Storage Fund grows in relation to the amount of data stored, which effectively takes more SUI out of circulation.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The Sui Network&#x2019;s capped total supply of 10&#x00a0;billion SUI tokens are unlocked according to a distribution and unlock schedule designed to balance liquidity, stability, and long<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-term</FONT> growth. The Sui &#x201c;mainnet&#x201d; launched on May&#x00a0;3, 2023 with a portion of the total supply made liquid at launch.</P>
		<P CLASS="H2" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">SUI Value</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="H4" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:1;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Digital asset trading platform valuations</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The value of SUI is determined by the value that various market participants place on SUI through their transactions. The most common means of determining the value of a SUI is by surveying one or more digital asset trading platforms where SUI is traded publicly and transparently. Additionally, there may be over<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-the</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak">-counter</FONT> dealers or market makers that transact in SUI.</P>
		<P CLASS="H4" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:1;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Digital asset trading platform public market data</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">On each online digital asset trading platform, SUI is traded with publicly disclosed valuations for each executed trade, measured by one or more fiat currencies such as the U.S.&#x00a0;dollar or euro or by the widely used cryptocurrencies Bitcoin and Ethereum. Over<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-the</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak">-counter</FONT> dealers or market makers do not typically disclose their trade data.</P>
		<P CLASS="H2" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">Forms of Attack Against the Sui Network</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">All networked systems are vulnerable to various kinds of attacks. As with any computer network, the Sui Network contains certain vulnerabilities. The Sui Network relies on a network of validator nodes that agree on the order and validity of transactions. These nodes form the backbone of the consensus process.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">If the malicious actor cannot control the validator nodes directly, they might attempt to compromise the validators that are already trusted by the network. This could involve hacking, bribery, deception or coercion.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">A malicious actor could also conduct an &#x201c;eclipse attack.&#x201d; In an eclipse attack, a malicious actor could isolate parts of the network so that the malicious actor&#x2019;s nodes can influence the consensus in isolated sections of the network, eventually leading to a split or takeover.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">This is not intended as an exhaustive list of all forms of attack against the Sui Network. For additional information, <FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">see &#x201c;Risk Factors.&#x201d;</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="H2" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">SUI Transaction Fees</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">In proof<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-of</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak">-stake</FONT> blockchain networks, &#x201c;Gas Fees&#x201d; also contribute to incentivizing validators who maintain the ledger and ensure the integrity of the network. Gas Fees are a fundamental component of blockchain networks, serving as a mechanism to compensate validators for processing transactions and executing smart contracts. These fees are required to allocate computational resources efficiently, prevent spam, and maintain network security. Gas Fees vary based on factors such as network congestion, transaction complexity, and the execution of smart contracts. The structure of Gas Fees is typically designed to balance affordability for users while providing adequate incentives for validators to secure the network and process transactions promptly.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The Sui Network splits Gas Fees into two parts: computational fees and storage fees. Computational fees cover the cost of processing transactions, set by validators each epoch through a reference price. Storage fees, paid upfront when creating or changing objects, go into a storage fund&#x00a0;&#x2014;&#x00a0;a pool that compensates validators for keeping data on<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-chain</FONT> long<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-term</FONT>. If users delete unneeded data, they receive a rebate from this storage fund.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The Sui Network employs a Gas Fee model that ensures predictable and efficient transaction processing while minimizing costs for users. Gas fees in the Sui Network are denominated in SUI and serve the following key functions:</P>
		<P CLASS="NL_m" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:48pt;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-24pt;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">1.<FONT STYLE="width: 20px;display: inline-block;">&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;</FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Transaction Processing</FONT>.&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;Every transaction on the Sui Network, including transfers, smart contract executions, and decentralized application interactions, requires a gas fee. This fee compensates validators for verifying and processing the transaction.</P>
		</DIV>

		<P CLASS="RRH" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:0;orphans:1;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:center;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin: 10px 0px 10px 0pt; page-break-after: always; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin-top: 10.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: 10.0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-align: center; font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: TimesNewRomanPSStd-Regular; color: black;">40</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:left;text-indent:0;widows:2;margin-top:8pt;"><A HREF="#TOC001">Table of Contents</A></P>



	<DIV CLASS="_idGenObjectStyleOverride-1" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;border-width:0pt;">
		<P CLASS="NL_m" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:48pt;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-24pt;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">2.<FONT STYLE="width: 20px;display: inline-block;">&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;</FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Resource Allocation and Network Efficiency</FONT>.&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;The Sui Network uses a unique transaction processing model that supports parallel execution, which optimizes throughput and reduces congestion. Gas Fees play a role in prioritizing transactions, ensuring that resources are allocated efficiently based on demand.</P>
		<P CLASS="NL_m" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:48pt;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-24pt;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">3.<FONT STYLE="width: 20px;display: inline-block;">&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;</FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Security and Spam Prevention</FONT>.&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;Gas Fees deter spam and denial<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-of</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak">-service</FONT> attacks by imposing a cost on every transaction. This mechanism helps maintain network integrity and prevents unnecessary strain on validators.</P>
		<P CLASS="NL_m" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:48pt;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-24pt;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">4.<FONT STYLE="width: 20px;display: inline-block;">&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;</FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Smart Contract Execution</FONT>.&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;Developers deploying and executing smart contracts on the Sui Network must pay gas fees to ensure that computational resources are allocated fairly and sustainably. The Move programming language, used within the Sui Network, optimizes execution costs and enhances security.</P>
		<P CLASS="NL_m" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:48pt;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-24pt;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">5.<FONT STYLE="width: 20px;display: inline-block;">&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;</FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Stability and </FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">Long</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">-Term</FONT></FONT><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;"> Sustainability</FONT>.&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;The fee structure of the Sui Network is designed to be predictable and user<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-friendly</FONT>. Unlike blockchain networks where fees may fluctuate unpredictably due to congestion, the Sui Network&#x2019;s parallel execution model and object<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-based</FONT> data structure help keep fees stable and efficient.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Gas Fees in the Sui Network are collected in SUI and are either distributed as validator rewards or utilized within network mechanisms to sustain long<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-term</FONT> decentralization. As network adoption grows and demand for computational resources increases, the gas fee model is designed to dynamically adjust to maintain efficiency and accessibility.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">Validators and Market Participants</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The Sui Network has three main groups of stakeholders. First are users of the Sui Network who submit transactions to create, mutate, and transfer digital assets or interact with more sophisticated applications enabled by smart contracts, interoperability and composability. Second are holders of SUI who have the option of staking their SUI to validators and participating and the proof<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-of</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak">-stake</FONT> mechanism. Holders of SUI also have the right to participate in the governance of the Sui Network. Third, and lastly, are validators who manage transaction processing and execution on the Sui Network. Validators earn rewards for processing operations. Users of the network hold their own SUI, which they can delegate to the validators of their choice as part of the validators&#x2019; stakes. In so doing, the validators reward users based on the amount of SUI they delegate. Users are free to withdraw their SUI or to change their selected validator when each epoch changes.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The Sui Network has developed technology to process blocks at high speed. Blocks are made and processed by validators in roughly 24<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-hour</FONT> time periods called &#x201c;epochs.&#x201d; Each Sui Network validator maintains its own staking pool to track the amount of stake and to compound staking rewards. Validator pools operate together with a time series of exchange rates that are computed at the beginning of each epoch. These exchange rates determine the amount of SUI that each past SUI staker can withdraw in the future. Importantly, the exchange rates increase as more rewards are deposited into a staking pool and the longer an amount of SUI is deposited in a staking pool, the more rewards it will accrue.</P>
		<P CLASS="NL_m" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:48pt;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-24pt;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">1.<FONT STYLE="width: 20px;display: inline-block;">&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;</FONT>Investment and Speculative Sector</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">This sector includes the investment and trading activities of both private and professional investors and speculators. Historically, larger financial services institutions are publicly reported to have limited involvement in investment and trading in digital assets, although the participation landscape is beginning to change. Currently, there is relatively limited use of digital assets in the retail and commercial marketplace in comparison to relatively extensive use by speculators, and a significant portion of demand for digital assets is generated by speculators and investors seeking to profit from the short- or long<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-term</FONT> holding of digital assets.</P>
		<P CLASS="NL_m" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:48pt;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-24pt;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">2.<FONT STYLE="width: 20px;display: inline-block;">&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;</FONT>Retail Sector</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The retail sector includes users transacting in direct peer<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-to</FONT><FONT CLASS="nobreak">-peer</FONT> SUI activity through the direct sending of SUI over the Sui Network. The retail sector also includes transactions in which consumers pay for goods or services from commercial or service businesses through direct transactions or third<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-party</FONT> service providers, although the use of SUI as a means of payment is still developing and has not been accepted in the same manner as bitcoin because SUI has a generally different purpose than bitcoin.</P>
		</DIV>

		<P CLASS="LRH" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:0;orphans:1;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:center;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin: 10px 0px 10px 0pt; page-break-after: always; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin-top: 10.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: 10.0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-align: center; font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: TimesNewRomanPSStd-Regular; color: black;">41</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:left;text-indent:0;widows:2;margin-top:8pt;"><A HREF="#TOC001">Table of Contents</A></P>



	<DIV CLASS="_idGenObjectStyleOverride-1" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;border-width:0pt;">
		<P CLASS="NL_m" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:48pt;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-24pt;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;"><FONT CLASS="Italic" STYLE="font-style:italic;font-weight:normal;">3.<FONT STYLE="width: 20px;display: inline-block;">&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;&#x00a0;</FONT>Service Sector</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">This sector includes companies that provide a variety of services including the buying, selling, payment processing and storing of SUI.&#x00a0;For buying and selling SUI, Binance and Bybit are some of the largest digital asset trading platforms by volume traded. For storing SUI, the SUI Custodian, is a digital asset custodian that provides custodial accounts that store SUI for users. As the Sui Network continues to grow in acceptance, it is anticipated that service providers will expand the currently available range of services and that additional parties will enter the service sector for the Sui Network.</P>
		<P CLASS="H2" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:99;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">Regulation of SUI and Government Oversight</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The Binance Complaint, the SEC&#x2019;s actions against XRP&#x2019;s issuer and the issuer of the TerraUSD and LUNA digital assets, as well as seemingly inconsistent views of different district court judges, underscore the continuing uncertainty around which digital assets are securities, and demonstrate that such factors such as how long a digital asset has been in existence, how widely held it is, how large its market capitalization is and that it has actual use in commercial transactions, ultimately may have no bearing on whether the SEC or a court will find it to be offered and sold as a security.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">As digital assets have grown in both popularity and market size, the U.S.&#x00a0;Congress and a number of U.S.&#x00a0;federal and state agencies (including FinCEN, SEC, CFTC, FINRA, the CFPB, the Department of Justice, the Department of Homeland Security, the Federal Bureau of Investigation, the IRS and state financial institution regulators) have been examining the operations of digital asset networks, digital asset users and the digital asset spot markets, with particular focus on the extent to which digital assets can be used to launder the proceeds of illegal activities or fund criminal or terrorist enterprises and the safety and soundness of spot markets or other service<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-providers</FONT> that hold digital assets for users. Many of these state and federal agencies have issued consumer advisories regarding the risks posed by digital assets to investors.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Recent events, including among others the bankruptcy filings of FTX and its subsidiaries, Three Arrows Capital, Celsius Network, Voyager Digital, Genesis, BlockFi and others, and other developments in the digital asset markets, have resulted in calls for heightened scrutiny and regulation of the digital asset industry, with a specific focus on intermediaries such as digital asset exchanges, platforms, and custodians.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">In addition, federal and state agencies, and other countries have issued rules or guidance about the treatment of digital asset transactions or requirements for businesses engaged in digital asset activity. President Trump&#x2019;s January&#x00a0;23, 2025 Executive Order, titled &#x201c;Strengthening American Leadership in Digital Financial Technology&#x201d;, aimed to reorient the federal governments approach to digital assets. The Executive Order emphasized the importance of the digital asset industry in innovation and economic development, and outlined policies to support the growth and use of digital assets, blockchain technology and related technologies. President Trump&#x2019;s order also revoked former President Biden&#x2019;s March&#x00a0;9, 2022 Executive Order, titled, &#x201c;Responsible Development of Digital Assets&#x201d; and the U.S.&#x00a0;Department of Treasury&#x2019;s July&#x00a0;7, 2022 &#x201c;Framework for International Engagement of Digital Assets&#x201d; and all policies, directives and guidance issued pursuant to those items produced by the previous administration.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">On January&#x00a0;21, 2025, the SEC&#x2019;s acting Chairman Mark T.&#x00a0;Uyeda announced the SEC Crypto Task Force. The task force has an objective of developing a comprehensive and clear regulatory framework for crypto assets. The task force also seeks to establish a practical and achievable process for registration of digital assets and design clearly defined disclosure requirements and frameworks.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">Various foreign jurisdictions have, and may continue to, in the near future, adopt laws, regulations or directives that affect the Sui Network, the SUI markets, and their users, particularly SUI spot markets and service providers that fall within such jurisdictions&#x2019; regulatory scope. Foreign jurisdictions including Canada, Germany, Sweden and Switzerland have also approved exchange<FONT CLASS="nobreak">-traded</FONT> SUI products.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">The effect of any future regulatory change on SUI is impossible to predict, but such change could be substantial and adverse to the Company.</P>
		</DIV>

		<P CLASS="RRH" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:0;orphans:1;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:center;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin: 10px 0px 10px 0pt; page-break-after: always; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin-top: 10.0pt; margin-right: 0in; margin-bottom: 10.0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-align: center; font-size: 10.0pt; font-family: TimesNewRomanPSStd-Regular; color: black;">42</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:left;text-indent:0;widows:2;margin-top:8pt;"><A HREF="#TOC001">Table of Contents</A></P>




	<DIV CLASS="_idGenObjectStyleOverride-1" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;border-width:0pt;">
		<P CLASS="H1" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:12pt;orphans:1;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-before:auto;text-align:center;text-indent:0;widows:1;margin-top:12pt;"><A NAME="T8"></A><FONT CLASS="Bold" STYLE="font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;">USE OF PROCEEDS</FONT></P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">We will not receive any proceeds from the sale of Common Stock by the Selling Stockholder pursuant to this prospectus. However, we may receive up to $500&#x00a0;million in aggregate gross proceeds from the Selling Stockholder under the PEF Agreement in connection with sales of shares of our Common Stock to the Selling Stockholder pursuant to the PEF Agreement at varying purchase prices after the date of this prospectus. However, the actual proceeds from sales, if any, under the PEF Agreement, may be less than this amount depending on the number of shares of our Common Stock sold to the Selling Stockholder and the price at which such shares are sold.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">We intend to use the proceeds from the sale of Common Stock under the PEF Agreement, if any, primarily for general corporate purposes, including the acquisition of SUI, unless otherwise indicated in the applicable prospectus supplement. General corporate purposes may include working capital and capital expenditures, research and development expenses, general and administrative expenses and potential acquisition of, or investment in, companies, technologies, products or assets that complement our business. We have not determined the amount of net proceeds to be used specifically for such purposes. As a result, management will retain broad discretion over the allocation of the net proceeds of any offering.</P>
		<P CLASS="Text_flush" STYLE="margin:0;padding:0;border-width:0;font-family:Times New Roman PS Std, serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;font-weight:normal;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;margin-top:8pt;orphans:2;page-break-after:auto;page-break-before:auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:0;widows:3;margin-top:8pt;">We will generally bear all costs, expenses and fees in connection with the registration of the Common Stock offered by the Selling Securityholder pursuant to this prospectus, but the Selling Securityholder will bear all incremental selling expenses, including commissions, brokerage fees and other similar selling expenses.</P>
		</DIV>

For additional information regarding the shares of our Common Stock included in this prospectus, see the section titled &#x201c;PEF Financing&#x201d; above. Except for the transactions contemplated by the PEF Agreement and the Registration Rights Agreement and as set forth in the section titled &#x201c;Plan of Distribution (Conflict of Interest)&#x201d; in this prospectus, A.G.P. has not had any material relationship with us within the past three&#x00a0;years. As used in this prospectus, the term &#x201c;selling stockholder&#x201d; means A.G.P.</P>

The selling stockholder may sell some, all or none of the shares being offered for resale in this offering. We do not know how long the selling stockholder will hold the shares before selling them and, except as set forth in the section titled &#x201c;Plan of Distribution (Conflict of Interest)&#x201d; in this prospectus, we are not aware of any existing arrangements between the selling stockholder and any other stockholder, broker, dealer, underwriter or agent relating to the sale or distribution of the shares of our Common Stock being offered for resale by this prospectus.</P>
